<tr bgcolor="#dcebf4">
<td align="left" valign="top" width="22%">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; COLOR: #296dc1; FONT-SIZE: 9pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Supplemental information</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; COLOR: #296dc1; FONT-SIZE: 9pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">regarding plan of</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; COLOR: #296dc1; FONT-SIZE: 9pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">distribution; conflicts of</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; COLOR: #296dc1; FONT-SIZE: 9pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">interest:</font></div>
</td>
<td align="left" valign="top" width="65%">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt">Under the terms of a distribution agreement, RBCCM, an affiliate of Royal Bank of Canada, will purchase the <font style="DISPLAY: inline">securities</font> from Royal Bank of Canada for distribution to MSSB.&#160;&#160;RBCCM will act as agent for the securities and will receive a fee of $0.175 per $10 stated principal amount and will pay to MSSB a fixed sales commission of $0.125 for each of the <font style="DISPLAY: inline">securities</font> they sell.&#160;&#160;Of the $0.175 per $10 stated principal amount received by RBCCM, RBCCM will pay MSSB a structuring fee of $0.05 for each security.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt">MSSB may reclaim selling concessions allowed to individual brokers within MSSB in connection with the offering if, within 30 days of the offering, Royal Bank of Canada repurchases the securities distributed by those brokers.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt">&#160;</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt">Delivery of the securities will be made against payment for the securities on October 8, 2014, which is the third business day following the pricing date (this settlement cycle being referred to as &#8220;T+3&#8221;).</font></font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt">&#160;</font></div>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt">In addition, RBCCM or another of its affiliates or agents may use this document in market-making transactions after the initial sale of the <font style="DISPLAY: inline">securities</font>, but is under no obligation to do so and may discontinue any market-making activities at any time without notice.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt">The value of the securities shown on your account statement may be based on RBCCM&#8217;s estimate of the value of the securities if RBCCM or another of our affiliates were to make a market in the securities (which it is not obligated to do).&#160;&#160;That estimate will be based on the price that RBCCM may pay for the securities in light of then prevailing market conditions, our creditworthiness and transaction costs. For an initial period of approximately six months, the value of the securities that may be shown on your account statement is expected to be higher than RBCCM&#8217;s estimated value of the securities at that time.&#160;&#160;This is because the estimated value of the securities will not include the agent&#8217;s commission and our hedging costs and profits; however, the value of the securities shown on your account statement during that period is initially expected to be a higher amount, reflecting the addition of the agent&#8217;s commission and our estimated costs and profits from hedging the securities.&#160;&#160;This excess is expected to decrease over time until the end of this period, and we reserve the right to shorten this period. After this period, if RBCCM repurchases your securities, it expects to do so at prices that reflect its estimated value.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt">For additional information as to the relationship between us and RBCCM, please see the section &#8220;Plan of Distribution&#8212;Conflicts of Interest&#8221; in the accompanying prospectus.</font></div>
</td>
</tr><tr bgcolor="#dcebf4">
<td valign="top" width="22%"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">&#160; </font></td>
<td valign="top" width="65%"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">&#160; </font></td>
</tr><tr>
<td align="left" valign="top" width="22%">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; COLOR: #296dc1; FONT-SIZE: 9pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Structuring the securities:</font></div>
</td>
<td align="left" valign="top" width="65%">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial; FONT-SIZE: 9pt">The securities are our debt securities, the return on which is linked to the performance of the underlying stock.&#160;&#160;As is the case for all of our debt securities, including our structured notes, the economic terms of the securities reflect our actual or perceived creditworthiness at the time of pricing.&#160;&#160;In addition, because structured notes result in increased operational, funding and liability management costs to us, we typically borrow the funds under these securities at a rate that is more favorable to us than the rate that we might pay for a conventional fixed or floating rate debt security of comparable maturity.&#160;&#160;Using this relatively lower implied borrowing rate, rather than the secondary market rate, along with the fees and expenses associated with structured notes, reduced the initial estimated value of the securities at the time their terms were set.&#160;&#160;Unlike the estimated value included in this pricing supplement, any value of the securities determined for purposes of a secondary market transaction may be based on a different funding rate, which may result in a lower value for the securities than if our initial internal funding rate were used.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt">In order to satisfy our payment obligations under the securities, we may choose to enter into certain hedging arrangements (which may include call options, put options or other derivatives) on the issue date with RBCCM or one of our other subsidiaries.&#160;&#160;The terms of these hedging arrangements take into account a number of factors, including our creditworthiness, interest rate movements, the volatility of the underlying stock, and the tenor of the securities.&#160;&#160;The economic terms of the securities and their initial estimated value depend in part on the terms of these hedging arrangements.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block">
